<div class="request-description">
<div class="description">
  <h5 id="cadastro-de-credencias-do-usuario-para-gerar-o-token-de-acesso">Cadastro de Credencias do Usuario para gerar o Token de Acesso.</h5>
<div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parâmetro</th>
<th>Obrigatoriedade</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Descrição</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>name</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Nome do usuário</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>email</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>E-mail válido</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>password</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Senha de no minimo 8 caracteres</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Retorno</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>status</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>success ou error</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>data</code></td>
<td>object</td>
<td>Objeto contendo os registros ou os erros</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>

  	  <div class="row row-no-padding row-eq-height collection-item" id="fb98a4b7-db84-47ec-9716-411de8babf00">
    <div class="col-md-6 col-xs-12 section">
  <div class="api-information">
    <div class="heading">
  <div class="name">
    <div class="request-method-size-lg request-method-inline"><div class="request-method--POST request-method" title="POST"><span>POST</span></div></div><div class="request-name"><div class="heading-component heading-h4 heading-component--">
  <p>Gerar Token de Acesso</p>
</div></div>
  </div>
</div>
<div class="request-url-container">
<div class="request-url">https://pedfarma.herokuapp.com/api/auth/token</div>
</div>
<div class="request-description">
<div class="description">
  <h5 id="gera-o-bearer-token-de-acesso-e-autenticação-na-api">Gera o Bearer Token de acesso e autenticação na API.</h5>
<div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parâmetro</th>
<th>Obrigatoriedade</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Descrição</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>time</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>int</td>
<td>Tempo em minutos, que o Token permanecera válido</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>email</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>E-mail credenciado</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>password</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Senha credenciada</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Retorno</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>status</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>success ou error</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>message</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Mensagem personalizada de Sucesso ou Erro</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>data</code></td>
<td>object</td>
<td>Objeto contendo os atributos: <code>token</code>* e <code>type</code>* caso sucesso ou null caso erro</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>*<code>token</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>TOKEN de Acesso para utilizar na autenticação da API</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>*<code>type</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>tipo do tokem, sempre será: "Bearer"</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
</div>
</div>

    <div class="authorization-info" id="auth-info-">
  
    </div>

  <div class="api-information">
    <div class="heading">
  <div class="name">
    <div class="request-method-size-lg request-method-inline"><div class="request-method--PUT request-method" title="PUT"><span>PUT</span></div></div><div class="request-name"><div class="heading-component heading-h4 heading-component--">
  <p>Alterar Credenciais</p>
</div></div>
      <div class="lock-icon"><div class="pm-icon-lock pm-icon-lock-- pm-icon-lock--md"></div></div>
  </div>
</div>
<div class="request-url-container">
<div class="request-url">https://pedfarma.herokuapp.com/api/auth/credential</div>
</div>
<div class="request-description">
<div class="description">
  <h5 id="aletera-as-credenciais-do-usuário">Aletera as Credenciais do usuário.</h5>
<div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Headers</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Authorization</td>
<td>Bearer</td>
<td>Hash Access Token</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Content-Type</td>
<td>application/json</td>
<td>Object Json {"param":"value"}</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parâmetro</th>
<th>Obrigatoriedade</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Descrição</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>name</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Nome do usuário</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>email</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>E-mail válido</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>password</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Senha de no minimo 8 caracteres</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Retorno</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>status</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>success ou error</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>data</code></td>
<td>object</td>
<td>Objeto contendo os registros ou os erros</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</tr>

  <div class="example-request__snippet">
    <div class="request code-snippet">
      <div class="formatted-requests is-default" data-lang="curl" data-id="a228dae0-ee22-42b0-85d5-95681b44dcb1_0">
        <pre class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-snippet-wrapper" data-title="Example Request" data-content-type="example-request" data-id="a228dae0-ee22-42b0-85d5-95681b44dcb1_0" data-clipboard-target="#curl_0_a228dae0-ee22-42b0-85d5-95681b44dcb1" data-before-copy="Copy to Clipboard" data-after-copy="Copied"><code class="language-javascript" id="curl_0_a228dae0-ee22-42b0-85d5-95681b44dcb1">curl --location --request PUT 'http://local.pedfarma.com/api/supplier/7' \
--data-raw '{
    "nome_fantasia": "Volkswagen",
    "razao_social": "Volkswagen LTDA",
    "cnpj": "43.662.958/0001-50",

  <div class="name">

<div class="request-description">
<div class="description">
  <h5 id="cadastra-um-novo-cliente">Cadastra um novo Cliente.</h5>
<div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Headers</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Authorization</td>
<td>Bearer</td>
<td>Hash Access Token</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Content-Type</td>
<td>application/json</td>
<td>Object Json {"param":"value"}</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parâmetro</th>
<th>Obrigatoriedade</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Descrição</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>nome</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Nome do Cliente</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>email</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>E-mail válido</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cpf</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>CPF valido com mascara</td>
</tr>

<td>Telefone valido com mascara</td>
</tr>

    <div class="col-md-6 col-xs-12 section">
  <div class="api-information">
    <div class="heading">
  <div class="name">
    <div class="request-method-size-lg request-method-inline"><div class="request-method--PUT request-method" title="PUT"><span>PUT</span></div></div><div class="request-name"><div class="heading-component heading-h4 heading-component--">
  <p>Editar Cliente</p>
</div></div>
      <div class="lock-icon"><div class="pm-icon-lock pm-icon-lock-- pm-icon-lock--md"></div></div>
  </div>
</div>
<div class="request-url-container">
<div class="request-url">https://pedfarma.herokuapp.com/api/customer/2</div>
</div>
<div class="request-description">
<div class="description">
  <h5 id="altera-o-cliente-específicado-pelo-id-passado-na-url">Altera o Cliente específicado pelo id passado na URL.</h5>
<p><a href="http://local.pedfarma.com/api/customer/%7Bid%7D">http://local.pedfarma.com/api/customer/{id}</a></p>
<div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Headers</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Authorization</td>
<td>Bearer</td>
<td>Hash Access Token</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Content-Type</td>
<td>application/json</td>
<td>Object Json {"param":"value"}</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parâmetro</th>
<th>Obrigatoriedade</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Descrição</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>nome</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Nome do Cliente</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>email</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>E-mail válido</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cpf</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>CPF valido com mascara</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>telefone</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Telefone valido com mascara</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Retorno</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>status</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>success ou error</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>data</code></td>
<td>object</td>
<td>Objeto contendo os registros ou os erros</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<td>int</td>

    <div class="col-md-6 col-xs-12 section">
  <div class="api-information">
    <div class="heading">
  <div class="name">
    <div class="request-method-size-lg request-method-inline"><div class="request-method--POST request-method" title="POST"><span>POST</span></div></div><div class="request-name"><div class="heading-component heading-h4 heading-component--">
  <p>Registrar Venda</p>
</div></div>
      <div class="lock-icon"><div class="pm-icon-lock pm-icon-lock-- pm-icon-lock--md"></div></div>
  </div>
</div>
<div class="request-url-container">
<div class="request-url">https://pedfarma.herokuapp.com/api/sale</div>
</div>
<div class="request-description">
<div class="description">
  <h5 id="regista-um-nova-venda">Regista um nova venda.</h5>
<div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Headers</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Authorization</td>
<td>Bearer</td>
<td>Hash Access Token</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Content-Type</td>
<td>application/json</td>
<td>Object Json {"param":"value"}</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper is-expandable"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parâmetro</th>
<th>Obrigatoriedade</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Descrição</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>forma_pagamento</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Nome da Forma de Pagamento (Boleto, Cartão, etc...)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>parcelas</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>int</td>
<td>Quantidade de parcelamento</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>acrescimo</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>double</td>
<td>Valor de acrescimo</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>desconto</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>double</td>
<td>Valor de desconto</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>total</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>double</td>
<td>Valor Total da venda</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>status</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td><code>ativo</code> ou <code>cancelado</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>observacao</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Descrição de alguma observação</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>produtos</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>array</td>
<td>array contendo um ou mais objetos com o <code>produto_id</code> e <code>quantidade</code> de produtos vendidos</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cliente_id</code></td>
<td>obrigatório</td>
<td>int</td>
<td>id do cliente comprador</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Retorno</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>status</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>success ou error</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>data</code></td>
<td>object</td>
<td>Objeto contendo os registros criados ou os erros</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</code></pre>

    <div class="heading">
  <div class="name">
    <div class="request-method-size-lg request-method-inline"><div class="request-method--PUT request-method" title="PUT"><span>PUT</span></div></div><div class="request-name"><div class="heading-component heading-h4 heading-component--">

  </div>

<div class="request-url-container">
<div class="request-url">https://pedfarma.herokuapp.com/api/sale/14</div>
</div>
<div class="request-description">
<div class="description">
  <h5 id="altera-uma-venda-específicado-pelo-id-passado-na-url">Altera uma Venda específicado pelo id passado na URL.</h5>
<p><a href="http://local.pedfarma.com/api/sale/%7Bid%7D">http://local.pedfarma.com/api/sale/{id}</a></p>
<div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Headers</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Authorization</td>
<td>Bearer</td>
<td>Hash Access Token</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Content-Type</td>
<td>application/json</td>
<td>Object Json {"param":"value"}</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper is-expandable"><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Parâmetro</th>
<th>Obrigatoriedade</th>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Descrição</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>forma_pagamento</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Nome da Forma de Pagamento (Boleto, Cartão, etc...)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>parcelas</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>int</td>
<td>Quantidade de parcelamento</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>acrescimo</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>double</td>
<td>Valor de acrescimo</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>desconto</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>double</td>
<td>Valor de desconto</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>total</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>double</td>
<td>Valor Total da venda</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>status</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td><code>ativo</code> ou <code>cancelado</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>observacao</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>Descrição de alguma observação</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>produtos</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>array</td>
<td>array contendo um ou mais objetos com o <code>produto_id</code> e <code>quantidade</code> de produtos vendidos</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>cliente_id</code></td>
<td>opcional</td>
<td>int</td>
<td>id do cliente comprador</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div><div class="click-to-expand-wrapper is-table-wrapper"><table>

<th>Conteúdo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>status</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>success ou error</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>data</code></td>
<td>object</td>
<td>Objeto contendo os registros criados ou os erros</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
